Of these, 170+ are privately owned, 100+ are owned by the government and 2 colleges are owned by semi-government institutions. The top NIRF-ranked Engineering colleges are IIT Madras, IIT Delhi, IIT Bombay, etc. Admissions are based on popular entrance exams like JEE Main and JEE Advanced, AP EAMCET and MHT CET. Table of Contents Important Highlights of the Top Engineering Colleges in India 2026 Top 10 Engineering Colleges in India based on NIRF Ranking 2025 Eligibility Criteria for Admission in Engineering in India after Class 12th Tier 1 Engineering Colleges in India: Exam Schedules 2026 Top-Ranked Private Engineering Colleges in India Government Engineering Colleges in India Courses Offered by Engineering Colleges in India Top Private Engineering Colleges in India: Tuition Fee Vs Placement Package Offered Top Engineering Colleges in India under INR 1 lakh Most Popular Specialisations offered by Tier 1 Engineering Colleges in India Important Highlights of the Top Engineering Colleges in India 2026 Among the consistent top 10 Engineering colleges in India, based on NIRF 2025, IIT Madras on top, and some other IITs across India, followed by National Institute of Technology. To get into BTech colleges in India that are top ranking, it's better to have an overview of the fees, the types of public vs private institutions with their fee brackets, the common entrance tests for BTech. Predict your chances here: Engineering Cutoff Predictor Top 10 Engineering Colleges in India based on NIRF Ranking 2025 The NIRF ranks institutions across categories based on teaching, research, placements, diversity, and public perception. For engineering institutes, the weightage tends to be higher for research and teaching quality. These top 10 engineering colleges in India are all national institutes of importance, and only a few have shifted positions over the last three years, with IIT Madras being the exception, scoring 95 out of 100 in the teaching and learning resources parameter. Eligibility Criteria for Admission in Engineering in India after Class 12th The basic eligibility for the best BTech colleges in India is as follows: Candidates must pass Physics, Chemistry, and Mathematics in the Class 12 exam from a recognised Indian board. For the top IITs in India, it requires a minimum of 75% aggregate. For general engineering colleges, most state and private universities require a minimum of 45% to 50% aggregate in PCM subjects. Must appear for exams like JEE Main and Advanced, or check state-level entrances like MHT CET for engineering colleges in Mumbai, and other university-specific entrance exams. It may vary once the final placement report is out. Q: Is JEE Main enough for BITS Pilani BTech admission? A: No, BITS Pilani doesn't accept JEE Main scores for admission to the BE course. Birla Institute of Technology and Science, Pilani BE admission is based on valid BITSAT scores. Selection is based entirely on the candidate's past academic record, specialisation preference, availability of seats and score in BITSAT. Candidates, who have passed Class 12 in 2022 are only eligible to appear in 2023 and are eligible to apply for the BITS Pilani BE course. A: Thapar University CSE cutoff 2024 was 54620 for the General AI category students for admission. The first-round cutoff for the same stood at 32664. So, considering the 2024 JEE Main ranks, students aiming for CSE admission at TIET must target to secure a rank up to 54620 in case they belong to the General category in the AI quota. For other categories and courses, the JEE Main cutoff ranks will be different. 25AdmissionsCoursesFeesPlacementsCutoffCompareBrochureCommonly asked questions On Top Engineering Colleges in India 2026: Ranking, Fees, Courses, Admission, Placements Q: Is it easy to get into VIT Vellore for BTech course? A: Admission to the VIT Vellore B.Tech course is based on the VITEEE score. VIT Engineering Entrance Exam is a computer-based test conducted for a duration of 2 hours and 30 minutes. The VITEEE question paper consists of 125 questions. The questions will be based on Maths, Physics, Chemistry, English and Aptitude. The shortlisted aspirants are called for counselling and document verification. Aspirants need to pay a course fee to confirm their seat in the institute.
